## 1. System Overview

### 1.1 What is ReliefSync?

ReliefSync is a comprehensive disaster relief management platform that coordinates emergency response between multiple stakeholders during natural disasters.



## 2. High-Level Architecture

### 2.1 Complete System Architecture Diagram

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph Users["ğŸ‘¥ USER LAYER"]
        C[ğŸ‘¤ Citizens]
        N[ğŸ¢ NGOs]
        G[ğŸ›ï¸ Gov Agents]
        A[ğŸ‘¨â€ğŸ’¼ Admins]
    end

    subgraph Frontend["ğŸ–¥ï¸ FRONTEND LAYER"]
        REACT[React 19.1.0<br/>Vite 6.3.5]
        REDUX[Redux Toolkit<br/>State Management]
        LEAFLET[Leaflet Maps<br/>Geospatial]
        SOCKET_C[Socket.IO Client<br/>Real-time]
        WEB3[RainbowKit<br/>Wagmi + Viem]
    end

    subgraph Gateway["ğŸ” API GATEWAY"]
        CORS[CORS]
        RATE[Rate Limiter]
        HELMET[Helmet Security]
        AUTH_MW[JWT Auth]
    end

    subgraph Backend["âš™ï¸ BACKEND LAYER"]
        EXPRESS[Express 5.1.0]
        SOCKET_S[Socket.IO Server]
        CRON[Cron Jobs]
    end

    subgraph Services["ğŸ“¦ SERVICE LAYER"]
        AUTH_SVC[Auth Service]
        USER_SVC[User Service]
        DISASTER_SVC[Disaster Service]
        NGO_SVC[NGO Service]
        AGENT_SVC[Agent Service]
        QR_SVC[QR Code Service]
        NOTIFY_SVC[Notification Service]
        PAYMENT_SVC[Payment Service]
        WEATHER_SVC[Weather/ML Service]
    end

    subgraph Database["ğŸ’¾ DATA LAYER"]
        MONGO[(MongoDB Atlas)]
    end

    subgraph External["ğŸŒ EXTERNAL SERVICES"]
        GEE[Google Earth Engine]
        FLOOD[Flood ML API]
        WILDFIRE[Wildfire ML API]
        DROUGHT[Drought ML API]
        EARTHQUAKE[Earthquake ML API]
        CLOUDINARY[Cloudinary CDN]
        PINATA[Pinata IPFS]
        RAZORPAY[Razorpay]
        ONESIGNAL[OneSignal]
        MAILERSEND[MailerSend]
        GOOGLE_AUTH[Google OAuth]
        GROQ[Groq AI]
    end

    Users --> Frontend
    Frontend --> Gateway
    Gateway --> Backend
    Backend --> Services
    Services --> Database
    Services --> External
    SOCKET_C <--> SOCKET_S
```

## 4. Frontend Architecture

### 4.1 React Application Structure

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph Entry["ğŸ“ ENTRY POINT"]
        MAIN[main.jsx]
    end

    subgraph Providers["ğŸ”§ PROVIDER HIERARCHY"]
        STRICT[StrictMode]
        REDUX_P[Redux Provider]
        PERSIST_G[PersistGate]
        BROWSER_R[BrowserRouter]
        HEROUI_P[HeroUIProvider]
        WALLET_P[WalletProvider]
        TOAST[ToastContainer]
    end

    subgraph App["ğŸ“± APPLICATION"]
        APP_JSX[App.jsx]
        ROUTER[Router/index.jsx]
    end

    subgraph Layouts["ğŸ“ LAYOUTS"]
        MAIN_L[MainLayout]
        AUTH_L[AuthLayout]
        DASH_L[DashboardLayout]
    end

    subgraph Pages["ğŸ“„ PAGES BY ROLE"]
        ADMIN_P[AdminPages]
        CITIZEN_P[CitizenPages]
        NGO_P[NGOPages]
        GOV_P[Gov_AgencyPages]
        AUTH_P[AuthPages]
        COMMON_P[CommonPages]
    end

    MAIN --> STRICT
    STRICT --> REDUX_P
    REDUX_P --> PERSIST_G
    PERSIST_G --> BROWSER_R
    BROWSER_R --> HEROUI_P
    HEROUI_P --> WALLET_P
    WALLET_P --> APP_JSX
    WALLET_P --> TOAST
    APP_JSX --> ROUTER
    ROUTER --> MAIN_L
    ROUTER --> AUTH_L
    ROUTER --> DASH_L
    MAIN_L --> ADMIN_P
    MAIN_L --> CITIZEN_P
    MAIN_L --> NGO_P
    MAIN_L --> GOV_P
    AUTH_L --> AUTH_P
    DASH_L --> COMMON_P
```

## 5. Backend Architecture

### 5.1 Express Server Architecture

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph Request["ğŸ“¥ INCOMING REQUEST"]
        REQ[HTTP Request]
    end

    subgraph Middleware["ğŸ”§ MIDDLEWARE PIPELINE"]
        STATIC[Static Files]
        CORS_M[CORS]
        COOKIE[Cookie Parser]
        BODY[Body Parser]
        HELMET_M[Helmet]
        MORGAN[Morgan Logger]
        RATE[Rate Limiter]
    end

    subgraph Routes["ğŸ›¤ï¸ ROUTE HANDLERS"]
        ROUTER[Express Router]
    end

    subgraph Response["ğŸ“¤ RESPONSE"]
        RES[HTTP Response]
    end

    REQ --> STATIC
    STATIC --> CORS_M
    CORS_M --> COOKIE
    COOKIE --> BODY
    BODY --> HELMET_M
    HELMET_M --> MORGAN
    MORGAN --> RATE
    RATE --> ROUTER
    ROUTER --> RES
```

## 6. Database Architecture

### 6.1 Entity Relationship Diagram

```mermaid
erDiagram
    USER ||--o{ NGO : "registers as"
    USER ||--o{ AGENT : "registers as"
    USER ||--o{ EMERGENCY : "creates"
    USER ||--o{ AREA_DISASTER : "reports"
    USER ||--o{ QR_CODE : "generates"
    USER ||--o{ FEEDBACK : "submits"
    
    NGO ||--o{ EMERGENCY : "responds to"
    AGENT ||--o{ EMERGENCY : "handles"
    
    COORDINATE ||--o{ PREDICTION_DATA : "generates"

    USER {
        ObjectId _id PK
        String firstName
        String lastName
        String email UK
        String password
        String googleId
        String role
        String phone
        Boolean verified
        String profile
        Boolean ngo_verified
        Boolean agent_verified
        Number helpRequestLimit
        Number requestLimit
        Number urgencyLimit
    }

    NGO {
        ObjectId _id PK
        ObjectId userId FK
        String ngo_Name
        String registrationNumber
        String registrationType
        String officialEmail
        Boolean status
        Boolean emergency
        Boolean is_verified
    }

    AGENT {
        ObjectId _id PK
        ObjectId userId FK
        String name
        String official_id
        String department
        String badge_number
        Boolean status
        Boolean emergency
        Boolean is_verified
    }

    PREDICTION_DATA {
        ObjectId _id PK
        Number latitude
        Number longitude
        String disasterType
        Number riskLevel
        String severity
    }

    QR_CODE {
        ObjectId _id PK
        ObjectId userId FK
        Number id
        String qrCodeUrl
        String tokenHash
    }
```


### 6.2 Database Schema Overview


## 7. AI/ML Pipeline Architecture

### 7.1 Disaster Prediction System

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph Input["ğŸ“ INPUT LAYER"]
        COORDS[User Coordinates<br/>lat, lng]
        CRON_TRIGGER[Cron Job Trigger<br/>Every 10 days]
    end

    subgraph GEE["ğŸŒ GOOGLE EARTH ENGINE"]
        CHIRPS[CHIRPS Dataset<br/>Rainfall Data]
        SRTM[SRTM Dataset<br/>Elevation & Slope]
        JRC[JRC Dataset<br/>Water Bodies]
    end

    subgraph Processing["âš™ï¸ DATA PROCESSING"]
        RAINFALL[getRainfall<br/>Monthly precipitation]
        ELEVATION[getElevation<br/>Terrain height]
        SLOPE[getSlope<br/>Terrain gradient]
        WATER_DIST[getWaterDistance<br/>Distance to water]
    end

    subgraph ML_APIs["ğŸ¤– ML PREDICTION APIs"]
        FLOOD_API[Flood Prediction API<br/>FLOOD_API/predict]
        WILDFIRE_API[Wildfire Prediction API<br/>WILDFIRE_API/predict]
        DROUGHT_API[Drought Prediction API<br/>DROUGHT_API/predict]
        EARTHQUAKE_API[Earthquake Prediction API<br/>EARTHQUAKE_API/predict]
    end

    subgraph Output["ğŸ“Š OUTPUT"]
        PREDICTION_DB[(Prediction Data<br/>MongoDB)]
        NOTIFICATION[Push Notification<br/>OneSignal]
    end

    COORDS --> GEE
    CRON_TRIGGER --> GEE
    
    GEE --> CHIRPS
    GEE --> SRTM
    GEE --> JRC
    
    CHIRPS --> RAINFALL
    SRTM --> ELEVATION
    SRTM --> SLOPE
    JRC --> WATER_DIST
    
    RAINFALL --> FLOOD_API
    ELEVATION --> FLOOD_API
    SLOPE --> FLOOD_API
    WATER_DIST --> FLOOD_API
    
    COORDS --> WILDFIRE_API
    COORDS --> DROUGHT_API
    COORDS --> EARTHQUAKE_API
    
    FLOOD_API --> PREDICTION_DB
    WILDFIRE_API --> PREDICTION_DB
    DROUGHT_API --> PREDICTION_DB
    EARTHQUAKE_API --> PREDICTION_DB
    
    PREDICTION_DB --> NOTIFICATION
```

## 8. Real-Time Communication

### 8.1 Socket.IO Architecture

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph Clients["ğŸ‘¥ CONNECTED CLIENTS"]
        C1[Citizen Browser]
        C2[NGO Dashboard]
        C3[Gov Agent Panel]
        C4[Admin Console]
    end

    subgraph Server["ğŸ–¥ï¸ SOCKET.IO SERVER"]
        HTTP[HTTP Server]
        SOCKET[Socket.IO Instance]
        EVENTS[Event Handlers]
    end

    subgraph Events["ğŸ“¡ EVENT TYPES"]
        DISASTER[disaster:new<br/>New disaster report]
        EMERGENCY[emergency:sos<br/>SOS alert]
        STATUS[status:update<br/>Relief status change]
        NOTIFY[notification:push<br/>Push notification]
    end

    subgraph Database["ğŸ’¾ DATA PERSISTENCE"]
        MONGO[(MongoDB)]
    end

    C1 <--> SOCKET
    C2 <--> SOCKET
    C3 <--> SOCKET
    C4 <--> SOCKET
    
    HTTP --> SOCKET
    SOCKET --> EVENTS
    
    EVENTS --> DISASTER
    EVENTS --> EMERGENCY
    EVENTS --> STATUS
    EVENTS --> NOTIFY
    
    EVENTS --> MONGO
```

## 10. Security Architecture

### 10.1 Security Layers

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph Client["ğŸ–¥ï¸ CLIENT SECURITY"]
        HTTPS[HTTPS Only]
        TOKEN_STORE[Secure Token Storage]
        INPUT_VAL[Input Validation<br/>Zod Schema]
    end

    subgraph Gateway["ğŸ” API GATEWAY SECURITY"]
        CORS_SEC[CORS Policy]
        RATE_LIMIT[Rate Limiting<br/>100 req/hour]
        HELMET_SEC[Helmet Headers]
    end

    subgraph Auth["ğŸ”‘ AUTHENTICATION"]
        JWT_AUTH[JWT Tokens]
        BCRYPT[bcrypt Hashing]
        OTP[OTP Verification]
        BLACKLIST[Token Blacklist]
    end

    subgraph Data["ğŸ’¾ DATA SECURITY"]
        MONGO_SAN[Mongo Sanitize]
        FILTER_OBJ[Field Filtering]
        HASH_TOKENS[Token Hashing<br/>SHA256]
    end

    Client --> Gateway
    Gateway --> Auth
    Auth --> Data
```

## 11. Data Flow Diagrams

### 11.1 Disaster Reporting Flow

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as Citizen
    participant FE as Frontend
    participant BE as Backend
    participant GEE as Google Earth Engine
    participant ML as ML APIs
    participant DB as MongoDB
    participant NS as Notification Service

    C->>FE: Submit disaster report
    FE->>FE: Validate form (Zod)
    FE->>BE: POST /disasterReport/{type}
    BE->>BE: Verify JWT token
    BE->>BE: Check helpRequestLimit
    BE->>GEE: Get geospatial data
    GEE-->>BE: rainfall, elevation, slope, water_distance
    BE->>ML: Predict disaster occurrence
    ML-->>BE: prediction result
    
    alt Disaster Confirmed
        BE->>DB: Save prediction data
        BE->>NS: Push to NGOs, Agents, Admins
        NS-->>C: Confirmation notification
        BE-->>FE: Success response with details
    else No Disaster Detected
        BE-->>FE: "No risk found" response
    end
    
    FE-->>C: Display result
```

### 11.2 User Authentication Flow

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as User
    participant FE as Frontend
    participant BE as Backend
    participant DB as MongoDB
    participant MS as MailerSend

    U->>FE: Enter registration details
    FE->>FE: Validate with Zod
    FE->>BE: POST /auth/register
    BE->>DB: Check existing email
    
    alt Email Exists
        BE-->>FE: Error: Email already registered
    else New User
        BE->>BE: Hash password (bcrypt)
        BE->>BE: Generate OTP
        BE->>DB: Save user with hashed OTP
        BE->>MS: Send verification email
        BE-->>FE: Success: Check email for OTP
    end
    
    U->>FE: Enter OTP
    FE->>BE: POST /auth/verifyEmail
    BE->>DB: Verify OTP hash
    
    alt OTP Valid
        BE->>DB: Set verified = true
        BE->>BE: Generate JWT
        BE-->>FE: Success + JWT token
    else OTP Invalid/Expired
        BE-->>FE: Error: Invalid OTP
    end
```

### 11.3 QR Code Resource Tracking Flow

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant NGO as NGO User
    participant FE as Frontend
    participant BE as Backend
    participant DB as MongoDB
    participant REC as Recipient

    NGO->>FE: Create QR code for resource
    FE->>BE: POST /qrcode/create
    BE->>BE: Generate JWT with resource ID
    BE->>BE: Generate QR code (qrcode library)
    BE->>BE: Hash token (SHA256)
    BE->>DB: Save QR record (TTL: 2 days)
    BE-->>FE: QR code data URL
    FE-->>NGO: Display QR code
    
    NGO->>REC: Provide resource with QR
    REC->>FE: Scan QR code
    FE->>FE: Extract token from URL
    FE->>BE: Verify token
    BE->>BE: Decode JWT
    BE->>DB: Check token hash
    
    alt Valid Token
        BE-->>FE: Resource verified
        FE-->>REC: Confirmation
    else Invalid/Expired
        BE-->>FE: Invalid QR code
    end
```

### 11.4 Voice Mail Emergency Flow

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as Citizen
    participant FE as Frontend
    participant BE as Backend
    participant GROQ as Groq AI
    participant FF as FFmpeg
    participant CLD as Cloudinary
    participant MS as MailerSend
    participant NGO as NGO

    C->>FE: Record voice message
    FE->>FE: Transcribe audio
    FE->>BE: POST /disasterReport/agenticSend
    Note over FE,BE: Audio file + transcript
    
    BE->>BE: Check urgencyLimit
    BE->>GROQ: Analyze transcript for emergency
    GROQ-->>BE: { conclusion, danger_level, reason }
    
    alt conclusion = "no"
        BE->>BE: Delete audio file
        BE-->>FE: "No emergency detected"
    else conclusion = "yes"
        BE->>FF: Convert WebM to MP3
        FF-->>BE: MP3 file
        BE->>CLD: Upload audio
        CLD-->>BE: Audio URL
        BE->>MS: Send email to NGO
        Note over MS: Includes audio link + transcript
        MS-->>NGO: Emergency email notification
        BE-->>FE: "Emergency reported successfully"
    end
```

---
